 On the occasion of his 71st birthday (70th anniversary), Bollywood megastar, Bollywood megastar Amitabh Bachchan said that he never paid attention to his popularity, but he also believed that someone's attitude towards life matters a lot
 pyaar se 'big bi' kahkar pukaare jane vaale amitabh bachchan ne ek saakshaatkaar main bataaya, "har insaan ko utaar-chadhaav se guzaranaa hota he
 
 
 Whatever comes up has to go down
 
 
 mujhe nahin lagata ki main kisi se alag hum
 
 
 We all have ups and downs in our lives
 
 
 " He said, "if you are successful, then you should keep in mind that it is not going to last long
 
 
 agar aap asafal ho rahe hai to aapako ladanaa chahie or vaapasi kerani chahie
 
 
 "in his illustrious career spanning over four decades, megastar Amitabh Bachchan, who has worked in nearly 180 films, said that his contemporary actors are also doing well
" bachchan ne kaha, "main apane bare main (lokapriy hone ke bare main) kabhi nirnay nahin letaa
 
 
 My contemporary actors lagged behind me
 
 
 aisa kahana galat hoga
 
 
 i never paid attention to my popularity
 
 
 log jo chahen, likh sakate hai, lekin mujhe isse fark nahin padataa
 
 
 "he named his old comrades that Shatrughan Sinha, Vinod Khanna, Dharmendra and Rishi Kapoor are still active in films, and unfortunately Shashi Kapoor is ill, otherwise he would have been active as well
" unhone kaha, "aaj vinod khanna or shatrughna sinha raajnneeti main pahunch chuke hai or acha kar rahe hai
 
 
 i feel that i have missed them
 
 
 " amitabh bachchan ne bataaya ki dilip kumaar or wahidaa rahamaan unke pasandida kalakaar bhi hai, or yahi donon kalakaar unke adarsh bhi hai
 He said, "when you talk about the history of Indian cinema, it can be divided into two parts
 
 
 ek dilip kumaar se pehle, or doosraa unke aane ke baad kaa
 
 
 " film 'shakti' kii shooting ko dinon ko yaad karte hue bachchan ne kaha, "jab aap apane priy kalakaar ke saath kaam karte hai to aapke man main bahut saare bhav aate hai
 
 
 He (dilip Kumar) is one whom i have seen since childhood
 
 
 jab ham donon shooting ke liye saath aae to mujhe thodaa ajeeb laga
 
 
 It was very difficult for me to digest that i would be seen on screen with Dilip Sahab
 
 
 main khushnaseeb hum ki mujhe unke saath kaam karne kaa mauka mila
 
 
 i am still in contact with him
 
 
 " Talking about his directors, Amitabh Bachchan said that he got the opportunity to work with many directors, but he considers Hrishikesh Mukherjee as his 'godfather'
 unhone khwaja ahamed abbaas kaa bhi shukriya adaa kiya, jinhone unhen unki pehali film 'saat hindustani' main kaam diya tha
 He said, "I consider Hrishikesh Mukherjee my 'godfather'
" 
 
 sabko lagata he ki maine prakaash mehara or manmohan desai ke saath zyaada filmein kii hai, lekin yah sach nahin he
 
 
 i have done more films with Rishi Da
 
 
 " He said, "manmohan Desai had a kind of madness
 
 
 vah darshakon kii nabz ko pahachaanate the
 
 
 Yash Chopra gave the biggest films of my career
 
 
 usee samay maine mukul anand or tinu anand ke saath bhi kaam kiya
 
 
 "comments amitabh bachchan ne karan johar, prakaash jha, sanjay lila bhansaali or shujit sarkaar jaise maujuuda or kadran nae nirdeshkon kii bhi tarif kii
 He told that he is working again with R
 Balki, Shujit Sarkar and Prakash Jha
 bachchan ne 'paan singh tomars', 'gangs of vasepur', 'viki donor', 'kahani' jaisi filmon kii prashansa bhi kii
 He said that these films were excellent and everyone liked them
 ullekhneey he ki amitabh bachchan ne varsh 1984 main raajnneeti main pravesh karne ke saath hi filmon se brake liya tha
 He became a Congress MP from Allahabad seat, though he quit politics after three years
 amitabh bachchan philhal chote parde par apane saphaltam tivi reality sho 'koun banegaa karodpati' ke chathe sanskaran kaa sanchaalan kar rahe hai
 Amitabh Bachchan, fondly called 'big B', told in an interview, "every human has to go through ups and downs
 
 
 jo bhi upar aata he, use neeche janaa hi hota he
 
 
 i don't think I'm any different
 
 
 ham sabake jivan main utaar-chadhaav aate hai
 
 
 " unhone kaha, "agar aap safal hote hai to aapako dhyaan rakhana chahie ki yah zyaada der tak nahin tikne vaali
 
 
 If you are failing you must fight and return
 
 
 " chaar dashak se bhi lambe samay se jari apane shandaar kariyar main kareeb 180 filmon main kaam kar chuke mahanayake amitabh bachchan ne kaha ki unke samakaleen abhinayta bhi acha kaam kar rahe hai
 Bachchan said, "I never make a decision about myself (being popular)
 
 
 mere samakaleen abhinayta mujhase peeche rah gaye
 
 
 It would be wrong to say so
 
 
 maine kabhi apni lokapriyata par dhyaan nahin diya
 
 
 People can write whatever they want, but it doesn't matter to me
 
 
 " unhone apane puraane saathiyon kaa naam lete hue kaha ki shatrughna sinha, vinod khanna, dharmendra or rishi kapur ab bhi filmon main sakriy hai, or durbhagyavash shashi kapur biimaar hai, varanaa vah bhi sakriy hote

 mujhe to aisa lagata he ki main unase peeche chhot gaya hum

 The past has always been full of differences
 ekta or ekajutata kii bajaae kalah-katutaa or bikharaav hi janata dal kii kundali kaa likhaa amit lekh
 Let us look at the scattered past of leaders associated with the foundation of the Janata Dal
 sangharsh ke sipaahi aaj milane ke liye nikal paden, phir se us ujde chaman ko sajaane jisaki raunak apane hi haathon se aksar matiamet karte rahe hai
 After the Emergency, when the Janata government was formed in the country, the fire of a quarrel in the Janata family from that time onwards, the dream of complete revolution of Lok Nayak Jayaprakash Narayan was shattered in front of his eyes
 satta kaa nasha kranti par kabiz ho gaya jisaki vajah se samaajawaadee kunba dhire-dhire jaateey golbandi kii siyasat or vanshavaadi guton main tabdeel hota chalaa gaya
 In the Janata government, there was a split between Morarji Desai and Chaudhary Charan Singh
 morarji kii sarkaar se alag hokar choudhary charan singh ne congress ke samarthan se sarkaar gathit kar lee
 The socialist clan of the Janata Party also fell apart after the fall of the Janata government
 jise jahaan raajnneeti kaa rasta mila wo usee party ke jariye raajnneeti karne laga or aakhir main rajeev gandhi sarkaar ke vakt boforce kii top se nikle ghotaale ke kathith jinn ne nae sire se janata parivaar ko ekajute hone kaa mauka diya
 When the finance minister in the Rajiv government, Vishwanath Pratap Singh rebelled against the Congress, all the young Turks came under his umbrella
 janata dal kii buniyaad pad gai
 On 11 October 1988, the foundation of the Janata Dal was formed under the leadership of VP Singh
 janata party, janamorcha or lokdal kaa janata dal main vilay ho gaya
 But after the formation of VP Singh government, the first break in the Janata Dal was led by Chandrashekhar
 chandrashekhar ne alag hokar janata dal samaajawaadee kaa gathan kiya
 He became Prime Minister with the support of Congress
 haalanki chandrashekhar sarkaar chaar maheene main hi gir gai
 The name of Janata Dal Samajwadi was changed to Samajwadi Janata Party
 phir to vibhaajan kaa silsilaa hi chal padaa
 With the heartbreak in the Battle of Ahem, the party also went to pieces
 koi netaa idhar gaya to koi udhar
 Deve Gowda along with VP Singh, Lalu Yadav, Nitish Kumar and Sharad Yadav were trying to save the Janata Dal, but no idea worked
 janata dal se alag hue chandrashekhar or mulaayam singh yadav main bhi foot pad gai
 In 1992, Mulayam Singh Yadav split from the Samajwadi Janata Party and formed the Samajwadi Party
 1992 main choudhary ajit singh ne bhi janata dal se alag hokar areldi namaki nai party bana lee
 This was the second break in the Janata Dal
 1994main janata dal se alag hokar jorge furnandis or nitish kumaar ne samta party kii buniyaad rakhi
 This was the third breakdown of the Janata Dal
 1996main karnataka ke netaa ramakrishna hegade bhi janata dal se alag ho gaye, unhone lokshakti naamak nai party kaa gathan kar liya
 This was the fourth break of the Janata Dal
 1997main lalu yadav ne janata dal se alag hokar argedy kaa gathan kiya
 This was the fifth major break in the Janata Dal
 1998main naveen patnayak janata dal se alag ho gaye
 The BJD was formed in Odisha
 ye janata dal kii chhathi badi tut thi
 In 1999, the remaining Janata Dal also became two parts
 devegoda kii aguwai main janata dal secular or sharad yadav kii aguwai main janata dal united
 This was the seventh chapter of the split in which the Janata Dal's existence ended forever
 to ye thi janata dal kii yatra ke aakhri padaav tak pahunchane kii choti si kahani

 ) uttar pradesh main yogi adityanath ke khilaaf satta virdohi rujhaan (anti inkambency) jor pakadta nazar aa rahaa he
 According to the Political Stock Exchange (PSE) data collected by Axis My India for India Today Group, Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath's popularity has declined significantly in the last 3 months
 kareeb do saal se satta main maujuud yogi kii lokapriyata kii tulana shivaraj singh chouhan or raman singh ke bataur madhya pradesh or chhattisgarh ke mukhyamantri tisare kaarykaal ke aakhri dinon se kii jaae to ye 6% kam dikhi
 Now that the BJP is gearing up for the Lok Sabha elections, the high graph of dissatisfaction against the BJP in Uttar Pradesh is causing a fresh headache for the ruling party at the Center
 india today ke liye exis kii ore se sitambar main kiye gaye pehle trekking pole main yogi adityanath kii lokapriyata 43% thi
 What is disappointing for BJP supporters is that in the latest survey conducted by Axis, Yogi's popularity has come down by 5% in the last three months
 disambar ke tisare hafte main kiye gaye PSE survey main sirf 38% pratibhaagiyon ne hi kaha ki agle siem ke liye yogi adityanath unki pehali pasand hai
 At the same time, Samajwadi Party chief Akhilesh Yadav, whose popularity stood at 29% according to PSE in September, rose 8% in the last three months to 37% in December
 akhilesh kii lokapriyata main oochaal ke baad ab wo yogi adityanath se 1% hi peeche rah gaye hai
 At the same time, the popularity of BSP Supremo declined by 3% between September and December
 mayawati kii lokapriyata sitambar main 18% thi jo disambar main ghat kar 15% rah gai
 The level of dissatisfaction against Yogi Adityanath can be understood only when the PSE figures of Uttar Pradesh are compared with the figures of Madhya Pradesh, Rajasthan and Chhattisgarh, where the recent assembly elections were held
 november ke PSE data main 44% pratibhaagiyon ne shivaraj singh chouhan ko madhya pradesh ke agle mukhyamantri ke taur par apni pehali pasand bataaya tha
 The same number of participants had described Raman Singh as their choice as the next Chief Minister in Chhattisgarh
 jahaan tak rajasthan kaa sawaal he to vahaan november main 31% pratibhaagiyon ne vasundhara raaje ko mukhyamantri ke ek or kaarykaal ke liye sabase pasandida ummidavaar bataaya tha
 This means that the popularity of Yogi Adityanath was 6% less than the popularity of Shivraj Singh Chauhan and Raman Singh who were out of power in Madhya Pradesh and Chhattisgarh
 rajasthan main mukhyamantri ke taur par apane kaarykaal ke aakhri dinon main vasundhara raaje kii lokapriyata se hi yogi adityanath aage dikhaai die
 The problem is not limited to Yogi Adityanath alone
 uttar pradesh sarkaar ke kaamkaaj ke khilaaf bhi asantosh teji se badhata ja rahaa he
 35% of the participants in the latest PSE survey said that they are completely dissatisfied with the functioning of the BJP government in Uttar Pradesh
 sirf 37% pratibhaagiyon ne hi kaha ki ve is sarkaar ke kaamkaaj se puri tarah santusht hai
 That is, the difference between fully satisfied and completely dissatisfied voters has come down to just 2%
 9% votaron ne kaha ki ve kuch had tak asantusht or 12% ne kaha ki ve kuch had tak santusht hai
 The PSE survey was conducted from 14 December to 19 December by Axis My India
 is dauraan uttar pradesh ke 80 sansadeey kshetron main telephone intervyuu liye gaye
 31,200 participants took part in it
 ye sample uttar pradesh kii aabaadi or bhugolic sthiti kii numaaindgi karne vaala tha
 The PSE data can closely identify the issues that voters are saying are most important to vote for in the 2019 election
 survey ke 32% pratibhaagiyon ne berogari ko sabase ahm mudda bataaya
 On the other hand, inflation is the most important issue for 21% of voters
 17% pratibhaagiyon ke liye kheti or kisaanon se jude mudde sabase ahm hai
 At the same time, only 9% of the participants considered hindu-muslim conflict
 mukhyamantri yogi adityanath par rajya main haalia chunaavon kaa sampradayik aadhaar par dhruvikaran karne kaa aarope lagata rahaa he
 PSE data indicate that the preferences may have been set wrong by Bahubali Yogi of Gorakhpur
 naa sirf rajya sarkaar kaa niraashajanak kaamkaaj bijepi ke liye chintaa kii baat he, balki vipakshi gathbandhan ke liye badhata samarthan bhi uske liye pareshaani kaa sabab he
 Nearly half of the participants in the PSE survey (47%) said that Samajwadi Party, Bahujan Samaj Party and Congress should unite in the fight against BJP
 28% pratibhaagiyon ne aise kisi mahagathbandhan ke khilaaf raay vyakt kii
 At the same time, one-fourth of the participants in the survey could not express a clear opinion as to whether the opposition should be a grand alliance
 PSE data main siton or voton kaa anumaan vyakt nahin kiya gaya he lekin isse ye saaf sanket miltaa he ki bharat ke sabase samvedansheel rajya main hawa kis ore bah rahi he
 If the popularity of a government falls below 40% before completing the second year in power, there is no good news for the BJP in the state
 bijepi ke liye uttar pradesh main sirf raahat kii baat ye he ki pradhanmantri narendra modi apni khud kii lokapriyata ko beete teen maheenon main badhaane main kaamyaab rahe hai
 In September, 48% of the participants expressed their opinion in favor of giving Modi another term as Prime Minister
 disambar main hue survey main 51% logon ne modi ko piem ke liye pasandida ummidavaar bataaya
 It matters a lot in itself that anti-incumbency has no effect on the Prime Minister
 beete teen maheene main congress adhyaksh rahul gandhi kii lokapriyata main bhi 4% kaa izaafaa hua he
 Rahul's popularity in September was 22%, which rose to 26% in December
 haalanki rahul ke samarthak utsaah main hai ki unki sweekaaryata bad rahi he
 But the reality is that even now there is a big difference of 25% between Narendra Modi and Rahul Gandhi in terms of popularity
 yani aglaa pradhanmantri koun? ke sawaal par modi rahul se kahin aage hai
 There is a strong concept among the people about the functioning of the central government, just as it is about the leader who leads the government
 PSE survey ke 52% pratibhaagiyon kaa kahana he ki ve centre sarkaar ke kaamkaaj ko lekar puri tarah santusht hai
 Only 29% of the participants said that they are completely dissatisfied with the functioning of the central government
 iskaa matlab centre sarkaar ke kaamkaaj ko lekar khush votaron kii sankhya is kaamkaaj ko lekar naaraaz votaron se 23% zyada he

 Besides the nuclear biological chemical purification system, the jammer station was also demonstrated during the parade
 chaak chauband suraksha vyavastha ke bich is baar kii parade kaa ek mahatvapurn aakarshan khoji kute the jin par dilli police kaa bam nirodhak dasta or rashtriya suraksha guard aatankwaadi ghatnaon or anya vaardaat kii jaanch main bahut bharosa karte hai
 Inventive dogs demonstrated a range of skills
 ganatantr diwas samaaroh ke liye suraksha ke chaak chauband prabandh kiye gaye or kisi tarah kii apriy ghatana se nipatane ke liye ardh sainik balon, dilli police ke javaanon ke alaava enesji ko tainaat kiya gaya
 Surefire shooters were stationed on the tall buildings, then closed circuit cameras were installed along with air surveillance from helicopters
 parade jis raste se guzar rahi thi uske aas paas kii har imaarat par suraksha bal chaukasee barat rahe the
 This time parade showcased aspects related to the development and historical and cultural heritage of the country through the presentations of 23 states and central ministries and departments
 rashtriya bahaduree puraskaar 2009 ke liye chune gaye 24 bacchon main se 19 parade main hissaa liya
 1200 students from two schools of Delhi and artists from various cultural centers gave colorful performances while 154 BSF jawans showed amazing performance on 30 motorcycles
 vayusena ke si-130-je super harculis vimaan pehali baar parade main shaamil hue
 The flypast was led by three Mi-35 helicopters at the conclusion of the parade
 unke peeche ek iel-78, do een-32 or do dronier ne akaash main bharat kii shakti kaa pradarshan kiya
 The comments iske baad, paanch jaguaar or paanch mig-29 ladaaku vimaanon ne akaash ke seene ko chirate hue ganatantr kaa jaighosh kiya

 ganatantr diwas samaaroh kaa samaapan raashtragan or akaash main gubaare chhodane ke saath hua

 nausena ke daste main leftinent manikandan ke
 148 soldiers under the leadership of Air Force and 144 other soldiers led by Flight Lieutenant Sneha Shekhawate in the Air Force squad saluted the President

 Before the parade began, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh, Defense Minister AK Antony and the three army chiefs paid tributes to the martyrs at the Amar Jawan Jyoti at India Gate
 iske baad raashtrapati ke salaami manch par tirangaa fahraate hi rashtriya gaan kii dhun ne sabko romanchit kar diya

 yah medal singh ke pita ne grahan kiya
 During the ongoing parade, 3000 km-long Agni-4 missile developed by the country's Defense Development and Research Organization, 150-km 'prahar' missile and unmanned aircraft 'rustom-1' were displayed
 dhwajarohan ke turant baad 21 topon kii salaami ke bich gajraj kii tarah aasmaan se mandaraate emai 17 helicopteron ne gulab kii pankhuriyaan bikheri to rajpath par baithe saikadon darshak mantrmugdh hue bina nahin rah sake
 Indian Army T-72 tanks, multiplexed rocket system, Pinaka multi-barrel rocket system and jammer station VHF (UHF) were also demonstrated
 sena ke unnat halke helicopter ‘dhruv’ ne akaash main swadeshi takneekee kshamta kii pataakaa fahraai
 The Indian Air Force demonstrated the C-130-J Super Hakrulis aircraft for the first time
 parade ke dauraan parmaanu jaivik rasinic shuddhikaran pranali ke alaava jaimar stesan kaa bhi pradarshan kiya gaya
 An important highlight of this time's parade amid the chalk-guarded security system was the investigative dogs on whom the Delhi Police's Bomb Disposal Squad and the National Security Guard rely heavily on investigating terrorist incidents and other incidents
 khoji kutton ne kai tarah kii dakshata kaa pradarshan kiya

 is baar kii parade main 23 rajyon or kendriya mantralayon evam vibhaagon kii jhaakiyon ke jariye desh ke vikaas or aitihaasik evam saanskrithik viraasat se jude pahaluon kaa pradarshan kiya gaya
